# CONCEPT 24 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "Trying not to overthink a video call with someone who makes me forget words."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for a lazy Sunday FaceTime date with someone new — trying not to overthink
**Register:** TENDER
**Duration:** 40 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Cross-blend 6+3 — sage green ribbed seamless set (tank + bike shorts) + open cream linen overshirt off one shoulder + bare feet + small gold hoops
**Hair:** HC-24 Claw-Clip Loose — twisted up casually with tortoiseshell clip, pieces falling
**Makeup:** ML-1 Bare-Glow — dewy nothing, tinted balm, brushed brows, cream blush tapped
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 7 — Shared Moment (bedroom floor, phone propped against books, afternoon warm-soft light, lived-in cozy with throw pillows, phone screen showing FaceTime notification)
**Music:** Lo-fi R&B bedroom pop, 88 BPM intimate
**Opener:** "He's calling in twenty minutes."
**Sign-off:** "...this is fine. Right? Okay."
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Through-mirror frame:** Frame 3
**Energy Arc:** Flutter (Frame 1) > Self-Soothing (Frame 2) > Amused Self-Awareness (Frame 3) > Soft Settling (Frame 4) > Ready-Not-Ready (Frame 5)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State (Bare Face, Stakes Declared)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Sage green ribbed seamless tank (fitted, comfortable, already wearing as loungewear). No bike shorts visible yet (she's sitting cross-legged so we can't tell bottoms). Cream linen overshirt draped over nearby chair arm (not on her yet). Bare shoulders visible. No jewelry. Phone visible propped against book-stack showing FaceTime notification on lock screen.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Messy post-nap hair — center-parted, slept-on waves creating slightly flattened areas at crown and extra volume at ends, some strands crossing face at cheek. Completely unstyled. Tortoiseshell claw clip sitting on floor beside her (ready to use but not yet). Authentic Sunday-afternoon energy.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Completely bare — post-nap face with slight pillow-crease mark fading on right cheek. Skin showing natural afternoon warmth. No product at all. Lips slightly dry (just woke from nap). Under-eye puffiness from sleeping. Natural and real and soft. This is the face she's worried about showing someone new.

HAND POSITIONS: Left hand pressing phone flat against books (steadying the FaceTime notification display, reading it one more time), fingers spread across phone back, thumb touching screen edge. Right hand at own cheek, fingertips pressing into right cheek in a "what-am-I-doing" self-aware flutter gesture, slightly squishing cheek creating dimple, ring finger near lip in thinking-touch.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — wide with flutter-energy (excited-nervous pupil dilation visible), looking at phone notification with slight panic-joy combination, right eye wider than left (surprise-dominant), catchlight at 3 o'clock from warm afternoon window at camera-left, amber flecks warm in golden light, slight crinkle at corners from suppressed nervous smile. Brows — both raised in "oh-god-it's-happening" expression, inner brows lifted creating soft worry-lines at forehead center, naturally ungroomed Sunday state. Lips — pressed into asymmetric nervous smile (right corner up in excitement, left corner held back in uncertainty), slight bite-mark visible on lower lip left side (she's been chewing in anticipation), lip-surface dry with natural color. Cheeks — right cheek squished by own fingertips (adorable self-touch), warm afternoon glow, pillow crease fading, no blush but emotional flush starting (pink warmth spreading from excitement). Jaw — slightly open from nervous-excitement breathing (faster than normal), chin tucked in cozy seated-on-floor posture. Breath — quick and shallow, chest rising rapidly with butterfly energy.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on bedroom floor (plush rug visible), cross-legged, surrounded by throw pillows (soft, lived-in, Sunday afternoon nest). Spine curved forward in casual cozy slump, shoulders asymmetric (left dropped toward phone, right raised from hand-at-face), weight settled into comfortable floor position. Bare toes peeking from cross-legged arrangement. Body language open but nervous — the flutter is in the details.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
Layer 1: Subject micro-action — right hand pressing cheek in self-aware gesture (caught mid-squish, cheek flesh displaced by fingertip pressure), left hand on phone just finishing a re-read of notification (thumb hovering as if to dismiss but not dismissing — keeping it visible), slight rock forward on sitting-bones (nervous energy micro-oscillation)
Layer 2: Fabric + hair state — messy hair strands at right cheek being pressed against face by her own hand (trapped between fingers and cheek), sage tank rib-texture catching warm light, rug fibers around her legs slightly compressed from body weight showing sat-here-a-while impression
Layer 3: Particulate layer — afternoon golden dust motes floating lazily in warm window shaft (15-20 particles, large and slow and Sunday-paced), one piece of lint from throw pillow drifting slowly upward from her exhale, warm and soft and domestic
Layer 4: Contact-point activity — fingertips pressing cheek skin creating visible dimpling and flesh-displacement, phone pressing against book-stack spine (weight and angle), crossed legs creating ankle-on-opposite-knee pressure point, rug fibers compressed under sitting-bones
Layer 5: Background motion — phone screen with FaceTime notification showing slight screen-dim (about to auto-lock timer, the urgency), afternoon shadows lengthening on bedroom wall through window (gentle time passage), throw pillow tassel swaying from her floor-sitting adjustment
Layer 6: Light in motion — warm afternoon golden shaft from large window camera-left, lazy and broad and soft (not sharp golden-hour yet, still diffused afternoon), slow dust-drift creating sparkle-field in shaft, phone screen adding small blue-white pool on book spines

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Throw pillows and rug texture in soft focus at frame-bottom and sides, creating cozy nest frame. A warm cream knit blanket edge. Bottom and sides 20%.
- MIDGROUND: Aira seated on floor, sharp focus, cross-legged with phone and nervous energy. Books with phone propped visible at her knee-level. Primary subject.
- BACKGROUND: Bedroom — warm walls (cream or soft clay), afternoon light through large window with sheer curtain (no direct sun, diffused glow), bed edge visible with rumpled duvet (she just napped there), bedside table with candle and earbuds case, pothos plant trailing from shelf. Lived-in, warm, personal.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Warm afternoon diffused window light from camera-left, soft and broad, 4500K warmth (afternoon not golden-hour), very gentle modeling with soft shadows, non-directional feeling
- Fill: Ambient room bounce from warm walls at -1 stop (well-filled, cozy, no harsh shadows), blanket and pillow bounce warming from below
- Rim: None prominent (soft overall lighting appropriate for tender register)
- Practical: Phone screen as small cool accent on books and fingers
- Light separation from BG: Subject barely brighter than background (+0.5 stop — she's IN the space, part of it, not separated from it)

FRAMING: Medium Close-Up (MCU) — top of head with 10% headroom (messy hair volume) to below waist (cross-legged position partially visible). Subject 65% of frame. Lookroom camera-right (toward phone/books). Camera height at eye level from floor-perspective (camera on floor with her — intimate shared-space angle). Body angle: 3/4 toward phone, face turning back toward camera for opener delivery.

LENS: 35mm (intimate environmental). APERTURE: f/2.8 — subject sharp with environment readable (the cozy space is CHARACTER here, not just background). Moderate depth. Bokeh: round, warm soft golden.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Celine Sciamma intimate domestic — the private tender moment before connection, shot from within the space (on the floor with her), warm and close without being intrusive.

ATMOSPHERE: Warm, soft, afternoon golden, light haze from dust-in-sunlight (level 2/10), cozy domestic comfort, grain Kodak Portra 800 (warm, slightly soft, intimate grain). Air quality warm and soft and Sunday.

COLOR GRADE: Highlights — warm soft gold, never harsh, gentle rolloff into cream-white. Midtones — sage green and cream palette, warm skin honey-gold, everything in soft warm family. Shadows — warm golden-brown, lifted significantly (no darkness in this space — it's safe), never cold. Overall reference: Sunday Afternoon Gold — Sciamma domestic warmth, soft and non-threatening, intimate without drama.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 2 — First Application (Tinted Moisturizer + Cream Blush)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

HAIR STATE (Frame 2): Same messy post-nap state, now pushed back from face with one hand (in between tucking and not). Slightly more intentional than Frame 1 but still loose and Sunday. No clip yet.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 2 — cumulative): Tinted moisturizer being applied — fingers spreading dewy light coverage across cheeks and forehead (sheer, luminous, barely-there coverage smoothing without hiding). Left cheek shows completed application (dewy glow), right cheek showing finger-streaks of product mid-blend. Cream blush dot visible on right cheekbone (placed but not yet blended — a salmon-pink circle waiting to be tapped in). Nothing else yet. This is the "I'm not trying too hard" look in active construction.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand at face, ring and middle fingers mid-blend on right cheekbone (tapping cream blush into tinted moisturizer base, fingertips with product visible), light tapping motion. Left hand holding small cream blush pot (open, showing salmon-pink cream surface), balanced on left knee (legs now extended in V-shape on floor), pot tilting slightly toward warm light.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking upward and slightly left toward bedroom mirror above dresser (checking work from floor position), soft dreamy quality to gaze (thinking about HIM while doing this), right eye catching golden afternoon light creating warm amber glow, left eye in softer shadow with catchlight at 8 o'clock from window reflection in dresser mirror above, lash fan visible from upward gaze. Brows — relaxed and natural, unbrushed but somehow charming, left brow slightly higher (hopeful-wondering expression), inner brows soft. Lips — genuine soft smile forming (unconscious — she's thinking about him while blending), right corner lifted more creating asymmetric tenderness, lips slightly more hydrated now (she licked them unconsciously), natural pink showing beautifully in warm light. Cheeks — left cheek showing dewy tinted base (luminous, fresh, Sunday-skin), right cheek with cream blush dot being tapped in (visible product circle being diffused by finger-taps), overall warmth spreading from smile and product together. Jaw — relaxed, soft, head tilted 5 degrees left (dreamy angle), throat soft and open. Breath — deep and relaxed (calming from Flutter of Frame 1 into Self-Soothing), chest steady.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on floor with legs extended in V on plush rug, weight shifted back (leaning on nothing — unsupported upright seated, core engaged casually). Slight slump-lean leftward. Linen overshirt off right shoulder creating casual asymmetry, fabric pooling around her like a soft nest-within-nest. Bare feet flexed slightly (comfortable, domestic).

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
Layer 1: Subject micro-action — right ring finger mid-tap on cheekbone (caught at contact-point, finger-pad compressing blush into skin, product spreading at tap-edge), head held steady with slight leftward tilt for afternoon light access on right cheek
Layer 2: Fabric + hair state — linen overshirt fabric catching warm breeze from cracked window (subtle rightward drift at hem where it pools on floor), hair strands across forehead drifting with same micro-breeze, tank rib-texture creating highlight pattern on torso in directional light
Layer 3: Particulate layer — afternoon dust motes lazier and larger now (8-10 in broad shaft), cream blush micro-particles on fingertip visible in macro (tiny salmon specks on skin), warm golden atmosphere thickening as afternoon deepens
Layer 4: Contact-point activity — fingertip tapping cheekbone (visible skin depression at each tap, product spreading in ring pattern from tap-center), left hand cradling blush pot on knee (pot warmth from her hand visible as slight product-softening at surface), bare feet on rug (rug fibers between toes, comfortable compression)
Layer 5: Background motion — phone still propped on books with screen now dark (timed out — building subtle time-pressure), afternoon shadow on wall advancing slightly leftward (time passing), sheer curtain billowing gently inward from cracked window
Layer 6: Light in motion — afternoon shaft slightly more golden than Frame 1 (time progression), cream blush on cheek surface catching and reflecting warm light as new glow-source on face, sheer curtain movement creating subtle light-variation as it filters/unfilters direct sun, dust motes moving through light creating sparkle animation

SPATIAL LOGIC:

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video (Opening)

SHOT TYPE: Medium Close-Up (MCU)
CAMERA MOVEMENT: Handheld micro-drift (lived-in energy, not polished), slight rightward drift, 8 seconds
LENS: 35mm
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s Aira on bedroom floor, cross-legged, phone in hand showing notification, wide-eyed flutter-face. At 1.5s she looks at camera delivering opener "He's calling in twenty minutes." At 3.5s she presses hands to own cheeks (nervous flutter gesture, "oh god"). At 5.5s drops hands, exhales, looks around room assessing herself. At 7.0s grabs cream blush from floor beside her (beginning).
LIGHTING: Warm afternoon from window, diffused, soft. Floor-level perspective. Sunday-cozy lighting.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Bedroom floor, throw pillows, rug, books with phone propped, afternoon warm light. Cozy nest. Sunday domestic comfort.
AUDIO: Music — lo-fi R&B bedroom pop enters at 0.0s at -10dB, 88 BPM, soft keys and muffled drums. Ambient — apartment sounds (distant traffic, neighbor's music faint). SFX — at 0.0s phone notification chime (the one that started it all — FaceTime scheduling sound), at 3.5s hands-on-cheeks gentle slap. VO — at 1.5s "He's calling in twenty minutes." (breathless, slightly panicked but happy, voice rising on "twenty minutes" in slight disbelief-excitement).
DURATION: 8 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, handheld energy creates organic micro-blur.
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: At 1.5s "He's" — H-breath + eez. "calling" — K + all-ing. "in" — short. "twenty" — T-wen-tee. "minutes" — min-its. Delivered with breathless speed, slightly rushed (nervous).
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 2 — Video (Application)

SHOT TYPE: Close-Up (CU)
CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slight push-in barely perceptible, 8 seconds
LENS: 50mm
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s Aira applying tinted moisturizer with fingers, spreading across cheeks. At 2.0s dabs cream blush on cheekbone (tap-tap-tap rhythm). At 4.0s pauses, tilts head, unconscious dreamy smile appears (thinking about him). At 5.5s catches herself smiling, looks down shyly. At 7.0s resumes application with renewed soft focus.
LIGHTING: Warm afternoon golden, soft on face, dewy products catching light beautifully. Intimate proximity.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Floor-level intimate, only her face and soft background visible. Cozy warm domestic ritual. The gentlest beauty routine.
AUDIO: Music — lo-fi continues at -10dB, melody becoming clearer (warm keys + soft vocal sample). Ambient — soft room. SFX — at 2.0s finger-tap-on-skin rhythm (soft, percussive, satisfying), at 4.0s her soft hum along with music (not words, just melody — she's relaxing into it). VO — none (the hum is enough).
DURATION: 8 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, finger-tap motions natural blur.
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: No speech. At 4.0s lips form soft unconscious smile (slow spread). At 5.5s lips pull inward in shy self-awareness. Gentle non-verbal lip dynamics only.
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 3 — Video (Through-Mirror + Claw Clip)

SHOT TYPE: Through-dresser-mirror from floor angle
CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static (observational, quiet, watching her laugh at herself), 8 seconds
LENS: 35mm
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s Aira's reflection in elevated dresser mirror, brushing brows with spoolie. At 2.0s she pauses, looks at herself, starts laughing (caught herself being too serious). At 3.5s full laugh — head thrown back slightly, genuine self-amusement. At 5.0s gathers hair up with both hands. At 6.5s twists and clips with tortoiseshell claw clip (practiced motion). At 7.5s shakes head testing clip-hold, pieces fall perfectly.
LIGHTING: Golden afternoon through mirror-reflection, warm everywhere. The laugh catching light. Most tender lighting possible.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Through-mirror domestic intimacy — bedroom visible in reflection depth, golden-hour building, the private moment of a woman laughing at herself for caring this much.
AUDIO: Music — lo-fi at -8dB, groove settling. Ambient — soft afternoon, birds outside window (gentle, Sunday). SFX — at 2.0s genuine laugh (soft, private, not performed — at herself), at 5.0s hair-gather whoosh, at 6.5s claw clip CLICK (satisfying snap-close), at 7.5s hair-shake swish. VO — none (the laugh says everything).
DURATION: 8 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, hair-gather and clip motion beautiful blur.
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: No speech. At 2.0s laugh begins (mouth opening, teeth showing, cheeks pushing up). At 3.5s full laugh (open mouth, eyes crinkled). By 5.0s laugh settling into soft smile for hair-clip action.
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 4 — Video (Lip Balm + Final)

SHOT TYPE: Close-Up (CU)
CAMERA MOVEMENT: Very slow push-in creating intimacy increase, 8 seconds
LENS: 50mm
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s Aira applying tinted lip balm directly to lips (casual one-hand swipe). At 2.0s presses lips together (setting). At 3.0s picks up mascara, applies one quick coat (fast, efficient, Sunday-casual). At 5.0s blinks, checks phone time. At 6.0s phone lights up — HE'S CALLING (earlier than expected!). At 7.0s her eyes widen (surprise-delight). At 7.5s deep breath visible.
LIGHTING: Full golden hour now — maximum warmth on face, lip balm and dewy skin catching every golden ray. Peak romantic light.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Intimate face-only, golden hour wrapping her. Phone visible at edge about to change everything. The moment before connection.
AUDIO: Music — lo-fi at -8dB continuing warmly. Ambient — golden-hour quiet. SFX — at 0.0s lip-balm cap off (click), at 2.0s lip-press (satisfying), at 3.0s mascara wand draw-out-of-tube (distinctive sound), at 6.0s FaceTime ringtone begins (the SOUND — iconic, recognizable, triggering every viewer's memory-association). VO — none (the ringtone IS the dialogue).
DURATION: 8 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, push-in smooth.
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: No speech. At 0.0s lips presented for balm (slightly parted). At 2.0s lips press together (setting balm). At 7.0s lips part in surprise-gasp (small O of "oh he's early!"). Non-verbal storytelling only.
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 5 — Video (Sign-off)

SHOT TYPE: Medium Close-Up (MCU)
CAMERA MOVEMENT: Handheld slight micro-drift (matching her nervous energy return), 8 seconds
LENS: 35mm
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s Aira looking at ringing phone, hand hovering over answer button, face caught between excitement and panic. At 1.5s she looks at camera (breaking fourth wall for sign-off). At 2.5s delivers "...this is fine." (not fine energy). At 4.0s "Right?" (genuine questioning, looking at viewer for reassurance). At 5.0s "Okay." (self-permission, deep breath). At 6.0s looks back at phone. At 7.0s her finger presses answer. At 7.5s immediate smile erupts — the BIGGEST smile of the entire concept — call connects.
LIGHTING: Golden hour maximum warmth. Phone screen adding green FaceTime glow to her golden-lit face. The warmest, most romantic light for the connection moment.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Bedroom floor nest, golden hour, phone ringing — everything leading to this press-of-button. The domestic space as the site of new-connection courage.
AUDIO: Music — lo-fi drops to -14dB (under phone ringtone). FaceTime ringtone at -6dB (PRESENT, urgent, recognizable). Ambient — quiet under ringtone. SFX — at 7.0s screen-tap (finger on glass — the decisive sound), at 7.5s FaceTime connection sound (the "bloop" of connected call). VO — at 2.5s "...this is fine." (voice slightly higher than normal, trying to convince self, nervous laugh in it). At 4.0s "Right?" (genuine question to camera, voice vulnerable and asking for permission). At 5.0s "Okay." (exhale-word, self-granting permission, settling).
DURATION: 8 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, handheld organic motion, finger-press at 7.0s decisive.
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: At 2.5s "this" — TH-tongue-through-teeth + is. "is" — iz. "fine" — F-bottom-lip + eye-n (said fast, clipped). At 4.0s "Right?" — R-tongue-pull-back + eye-t (rising intonation, questioning). At 5.0s "Okay." — Oh-Kay (exhale delivery, dropping tone). At 7.5s: lips SPREAD into wide genuine smile (no words, just joy-eruption as call connects).
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

---

# CONCEPT 25 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "Everything packed but me — one last sunset from this window before the door locks forever."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for my last night in this apartment — everything is packed except me
**Register:** REVERENT
**Duration:** 48 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Cross-blend 5+7 — deep midnight navy tailored jumpsuit, structured shoulder, gold zipper front + pointed black stiletto + vintage gold cuff + small black clutch
**Hair:** HC-14 Side-Sweep Cascade — all hair to right shoulder, left ear exposed with single gold drop earring
**Makeup:** ML-12 Smoky Eye Editorial — defined smoky eye, contoured cheek, nude glossy lip
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 3 reimagined as NEARLY-EMPTY APARTMENT (mirror leaning on bare wall, packing boxes stacked in BG, single floor lamp (no furniture), jumpsuit hanging on coat hook, sunset through curtainless window, dust from boxes in light shafts, melancholy beauty)
**Music:** Olafur Arnalds ambient strings + piano, 72 BPM melancholy
**Opener:** "Last sunset from this window."
**Sign-off:** "Okay... door locked. Gone."
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Through-mirror frame:** Frame 4
**Energy Arc:** Bittersweet Arrival (Frame 1) > Ritual Comfort (Frame 2) > Building Beauty (Frame 3) > Reflective Peak (Frame 4) > Armoring (Frame 5) > Farewell (Frame 6)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State (Bare Face, Stakes Declared)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Worn grey marl t-shirt (oversized, comfort-wear, moving-day clothes), black joggers rolled at ankle, bare feet on bare hardwood (no rug anymore — it's packed). The navy jumpsuit hanging on coat hook by door visible in background — the one beautiful thing not yet in a box. No jewelry, no shoes visible.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Loose, natural, slightly dusty from packing boxes all day (running hands through it repeatedly — stress-fidget evidence). Pushed behind both ears hastily. Not styled, not considered. Survival hair.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Bare face. Slightly tired — visible tiredness from the emotional-physical work of packing a life. Under-eye circles more prominent than other concepts. Slight dryness at cheeks from cardboard-dust. Lips chapped and bare. The face of someone who's been crying earlier and washed their face since. Pink at nose and inner eye corners (post-tears residue). Real and raw and reverent.

HAND POSITIONS: Both hands pressed flat against the bare window glass, fingers spread wide, palms against cold glass, arms extended forward. She's standing at the curtainless window watching sunset, pressing herself against the view one last time. Back partially to camera — we see her from behind at 3/4, face profile visible in window glass reflection.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking out at sunset through window (face partially visible in reflection/profile), slight squint from direct warm light flooding in, eyes glistening with unshed emotion (moisture visible at lower lid catching golden light), left eye visible in profile showing full lash-line and golden iris-edge catching sunset directly, distant-stare quality (seeing the view but also seeing all the memories in it). Brows — natural and soft, slightly drawn together at center in bittersweet expression, no anger or grief — just recognition of ending. Lips — pressed together in a line that holds back feeling, slight tremble at lower lip (micro, barely there), corners slightly downturned in wistful set, then beginning to open for opener line. Cheeks — bare, slightly flushed at cheekbone from emotion and sunset-warmth, post-tears pinkness subtle but present. Jaw — slightly clenched in emotion-holding, visible tension at masseter from trying to stay composed, swallow visible at throat. Breath — deep slow inhale through nose (chest lifting), the breath of someone gathering themselves to speak a truth.

BODY POSTURE: Standing at window facing it directly, weight 50/50 centered, arms extended forward pressing hands against glass (full body reaching toward the outside/sunset/what's-beyond), spine straight but with slight lean forward into the window (as if she could press through it). Head turned 20 degrees left giving us her profile and the window-reflection simultaneously. Bare feet flat on cold hardwood. The posture of someone touching something for the last time.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
Layer 1: Subject micro-action — hands pressing against glass with visible finger-pad compression (flesh whitening at tips from pressure), chest mid-inhale (expanding), head just beginning to turn from window toward camera (opener delivery about to happen — caught at 10% of turn)
Layer 2: Fabric + hair state — oversized t-shirt shifting with her inhale (fabric rising at ribcage), loose hair catching sunset from behind in amber-gold backlight creating halo effect, single strand crossing in front of face at cheekbone (covering and revealing)
Layer 3: Particulate layer — DUST FROM BOXES — thick visible dust motes in sunset shaft through curtainless window (25-30 particles, aggressive golden, large and slow-drifting), the apartment's memory released into light, some particles appearing to flow around her body creating air-current visible evidence, packing tape catching light somewhere
Layer 4: Contact-point activity — palms flat on glass (10 fingertips whitened from pressure, palm-flesh creating fog-circles from body warmth on cold glass, fingerprints appearing on glass surface), bare feet on hardwood (cool wood, toe-spread, floor scratches visible — the marks of furniture that lived here), t-shirt neck pulling at shoulder from arm extension
Layer 5: Background motion — through window: street life visible at distance (soft car headlights beginning to appear as evening approaches, tree silhouettes against orange sky), inside: dust settling in shaft (visible descent of particles), nothing else moves — the apartment is emptied and still, it has no life of its own anymore
Layer 6: Light in motion — SUNSET flooding through curtainless window at maximum drama (no curtain = no diffusion = raw golden-orange light in hard shaft), dust making light visible as solid beam-columns, light moving perceptibly across bare floor as sun descends (time passage visible in light-crawl), glass creating secondary specular points on far wall behind her

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Her body from behind/3/4, slightly soft focus on near-arm and near-hip (we're behind her at slight distance), creating voyeur-reverence energy, silhouette edge lit by sunset. 
- MIDGROUND: The WINDOW is midground — glass with her hands pressing it, sunset visible through, city beyond. Her reflection in glass is readable (face, emotion). This is the emotional center.
- BACKGROUND (through window): City at sunset — buildings catching last light, sky gradient from orange-gold at horizon to deep blue above, tree-line silhouette, the world beyond this apartment continuing while this one room ends.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Direct sunset through curtainless window, 2800K intense amber-orange, hard and unfiltered, flooding in as aggressive warm shaft filling 60% of room
- Fill: Sunset bounce from bare hardwood floor at -1.5 stops, warm reflective surface now with no rug
- Rim: Sunset creating extreme warm backlight on her entire silhouette (full-body rim) as she faces toward the source
- Practical: Single floor lamp behind her (off but visible — no other light sources remain), also the jumpsuit on hook catching sunset light as a narrative object
- Light separation from BG: She's IN the light shaft — not separated from it but part of it. Subject and environment unified in golden-orange flood.

FRAMING: Medium Shot (MS) from behind/3/4 — we see her from behind-left, showing hands on glass, profile visible, sunset through window. Top of head with 8% headroom to below hip. Subject 60% of frame. No lookroom needed (facing away). Camera height at mid-back (slightly below eye level from behind). Body angle: 170 degrees away from camera (mostly back-to-us), creating silhouette-intimacy.

LENS: 35mm. APERTURE: f/2.8 — subject sharp, window and sunset visible and beautiful, background stacked boxes readable in warm-dark edges of room. Bokeh: round, warm amber.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Terrence Malick light-worship — figure against window, light as character, dust as time made visible. The human against vast light. Also: Wong Kar-Wai farewell-space longing.

ATMOSPHERE: Heavy golden-amber sunset flooding, THICK dust (level 7/10 — the boxes have released years of accumulated dust into this one shaft), deeply melancholy but beautiful. Grain: Kodak Vision3 250D (medium grain, warm, cinematic) pushed to 500. Air quality thick with dust and golden light — you can FEEL the air.

COLOR GRADE: Highlights — blown amber-orange at window (full sunset clipping into warm white-orange). Midtones — deep amber-gold, everything in warm family, boxes in shadows reading as warm brown shapes. Shadows — warm brown-orange at deepest, lifted 5% (nothing is true black — even darkness is warm in farewell light). Overall: Malick Sunset Farewell — light as emotion, dust as time, warmth as memory.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 2 — Ritual Comfort (Base Application)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 2): Same grey t-shirt and joggers. Now seated on hardwood floor (no chair to sit on — all packed). A single folded towel beneath her as cushion. Makeup bag open on floor beside her — she's pulled what she needs from a packing box. Mirror leaning against bare wall in front of her. Bare feet.

HAIR STATE (Frame 2): Pushed behind ears for face access, still unstyled and dusty. Natural waves limp from long day. Not considered yet — functional only.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 2 — cumulative): Skincare applied (cleansed face, moisturizer, slightly refreshed from earlier post-crying rawness). Foundation being applied now — full coverage going on with brush for ML-12's perfected base, right cheek and forehead done, jaw being worked. Deliberate and meditative application. Concealer not yet. No eyes, no lips, no color.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding flat kabuki brush, pressing and sweeping along left jaw in slow deliberate strokes, brush angled with bristles fanning against jawline. Left hand holding small mirror (compact, propped against bent left knee) angled upward reflecting her face for detail work — the leaning wall mirror is for full-look checks, this compact for close work on the floor.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking down into compact mirror on knee, slightly meditative and calm (the routine is soothing her — familiar motion in unfamiliar empty space), right eye soft-focused on own jaw in reflection, left eye catching golden sunset side-light, slightly puffed from earlier emotion but calming. Brows — relaxed now (soothed by ritual), slightly drawn in focus but no distress, natural and soft. Lips — slightly parted in meditative calm, breathing through mouth slowly, corners neutral — neither happy nor sad, just present, accepting. Cheeks — right showing smooth foundation (evening out the post-crying pinkness), left jaw area being worked now with brush. Jaw — relaxed for application (muscles releasing from earlier clench), head slightly tilted to present jaw to brush, throat soft. Breath — slow and deep and rhythmic (matching brush-strokes, meditative pace).

BODY POSTURE: Seated cross-legged on bare hardwood floor with folded towel beneath, spine in comfortable curve forward toward compact mirror on knee, shoulders rounded inward (self-holding posture, comforting), right arm working at face, left holding compact braced against knee. Weight settled into floor position. Bare feet tucked under. Grounded despite everything being ungrounded.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
Layer 1: Subject micro-action — brush sweeping along jaw in slow deliberate stroke (caught mid-sweep, bristles creating product-wake on skin surface), head tilted slightly for jaw-access, breathing in rhythm with brush motion
Layer 2: Fabric + hair state — t-shirt pooling around crossed legs in comfortable-sad draping, hair strands at ear drifting with her exhale (leftward micro-movement), compact mirror in hand reflecting shimmering gold from sunset at angle
Layer 3: Particulate layer — dust from boxes still heavy in sunset shaft crossing above her (15-20 particles at varied heights, she's below the main shaft — sitting on floor), two particles catching compact-mirror-reflected light creating secondary golden points at floor level, paint-dust from old walls
Layer 4: Contact-point activity — brush pressing into jaw (skin compression visible at bristle edge), left hand cradling compact (mirror edge pressing into finger pad), bare feet pressing hardwood (cold floor contact — subtle toe-curl for warmth), towel beneath creating thin barrier from hard floor
Layer 5: Background motion — dust shaft above her moving slowly as sunset progresses (light crawling rightward on far wall), packing boxes in BG stacked and taped (labels visible but unreadable, this-end-up arrows), the emptiness of the room becoming more apparent as we see it from floor level — no shelves, no art, no life on walls (just picture hooks and lighter-colored rectangles where frames hung)
Layer 6: Light in motion — sunset shaft crossing above her at eye-level when seated (she's BENEATH the most dramatic light, in the calm below the storm), golden light crawling rightward on bare wall behind her, compact mirror occasionally catching shaft and bouncing warm light onto her face as secondary gold-fill (intermittent as angle shifts with her hand micro-adjustments)

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Hardwood floor in soft focus with makeup items spread (brush bag open, few products out on towel), her crossed legs partially visible. Floor-level intimate perspective. Bottom 20%.
- MIDGROUND: Aira seated on floor, sharp focus, applying foundation with meditative calm. Mirror leaning against wall behind her reflecting room back. She's small in the empty space.
- BACKGROUND: Nearly-empty apartment — bare walls with picture-hook ghosts and paint-color-difference rectangles where art hung, stacked boxes (3-4 high, labeled), curtainless window with sunset shaft above her, coat hook with navy jumpsuit hanging (narrative object waiting), single floor lamp in corner (off). The emptiness is character.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Sunset shaft crossing above her head-height (she's on floor, light is chest-to-head level), catching her face at golden angle, 2800K intense but only partially on her — she's at the edge of the shaft
- Fill: Hardwood floor bounce creating warm under-fill at -2 stops (floor is golden in sunset reflection)
- Rim: Golden sunset catching top of head and right shoulder as she's at shaft-edge, creating warm halo on hair
- Practical: Floor lamp (off), leaning mirror reflecting sunset shaft creating secondary warm glow
- Light separation from BG: Bare walls in shadow behind her are -2 stops from her face — she's brighter than the emptied space, still alive in it

FRAMING: Medium Close-Up (MCU) from floor-level — top of head with 8% headroom to below hands at compact-on-knee level. Subject 65% of frame. Camera on floor with her (shared level, shared vulnerability). Lookroom camera-right (toward compact mirror). Body angle: 3/4 facing compact, face directed downward into hand mirror.

LENS: 50mm. APERTURE: f/2.2 — face and hands sharp, floor items soft, background empty apartment in soft focus (but readable — the emptiness is story). Bokeh: round, warm amber from sunset light.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Wong Kar-Wai empty-apartment melancholy — the figure alone in a space that once held a life, beauty in the dissolution, warm light as memory. The small figure in the large empty frame.

ATMOSPHERE: Warm amber sunset cutting through dust, melancholy-beautiful, the room hollow and resonant (no soft furnishings to absorb sound — suggested by hard surfaces). Grain: Kodak Vision3 250D warm. Air quality thick with dust and sunset and memory.

COLOR GRADE: Highlights — amber-gold at sunset shaft intensity. Midtones — warm but muted (the apartment is beige and empty, warm light hitting neutral surfaces), skin as warmest element. Shadows — warm brown, slightly heavier than other frames (the emptiness has weight). Overall: Wong Kar-Wai Farewell Space — warm light in empty room, beauty of leaving.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 3 — Building Beauty (Smoky Eye Begins)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 3): Same grey t-shirt and joggers, seated on floor. No wardrobe change yet (makeup before dress for smoky eye — fallout protection).

HAIR STATE (Frame 3): Still loose and functional, now brushed smooth (preparation for styling), tucked behind ears fully for eye-work access.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 3 — cumulative): Full base complete (foundation, concealer covering under-eye tiredness, powder set, skin looking fresh and renewed). Brows defined with pencil (natural shape enhanced). Smoky eye IN PROGRESS — dark brown/charcoal transition shade blended across right lid and into crease (ML-12's editorial smoky building), left eye showing base shade only (lighter buff across lid, darker not yet applied). Working from right eye to left. No liner yet. No mascara. No lip. Contour beginning at cheekbones.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding blending brush (fluffy dome shape, loaded with dark pigment), swirling in left eye outer-V area, brush at 40-degree angle with visible pigment on bristle tips. Left hand at own forehead, pushing hair back and holding it (keeping strands clear of wet-shadow area), fingers fanned across hairline, forearm elevated.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — left eye half-closed for shadow application (lid relaxed, right-eye-completed smoky visible even in squeeze-closed position), right eye open and checking progress in leaning mirror across from her (distance-check, assessing blend-edge), smoky shadow on right eye creating dramatic effect even at half-complete stage, catchlight at 4 o'clock from sunset (now lower angle). Brows — right slightly raised in assessment, left neutral from closed-eye relaxation, defined with product now creating cleaner lines. Lips — slightly pursed in concentration, pushing toward right (cheek-distortion of focus), bare but less chapped (balm applied between frames as self-care). Cheeks — base smooth and fresh (tiredness hidden), contour beginning at right cheekbone (shadow placed, blending needed), apple neutral. Jaw — steady for eye-work, tilted 5 degrees right for mirror angle, neck showing tension of arm-elevated holding.

BODY POSTURE: Seated cross-legged on floor, closer to leaning mirror now (scooted forward), spine straighter than Frame 2 (more engaged, routine giving her energy), both arms elevated (one for brush, one holding hair), creating open chest posture. Weight centered on sitting bones.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
Layer 1: Subject micro-action — blending brush swirling in outer-V of left eye (circular motion caught at 3 o'clock position of swirl, bristles fanned from pressure), hair-holding hand keeping tension at hairline preventing forward-fall
Layer 2: Fabric + hair state — t-shirt rising slightly from double-arm elevation (midriff peek at right side), hair under left hand pressure smooth and held, loose ends at back drifting rightward from her body-heat convection current
Layer 3: Particulate layer — eyeshadow fallout particles (4-5 dark specks) on right cheekbone below eye (ML-12 smoky eye tax), box-dust in sunset shaft above her thinning as room settles (10-12 particles, still golden), one shadow-particle caught in descent from brush to cheek
Layer 4: Contact-point activity — brush bristles pressing into lid crease (skin folding at contact, pigment transfer visible), left hand spreading pressure across hairline (multiple fingertip pressure points, hair compressed), sitting bones on folded towel on hardwood (dual pressure)
Layer 5: Background motion — sunset shaft now lower and more horizontal (time passage), crawling light-stripe on bare wall progressed 30cm from Frame 2, boxes unchanged (silent witnesses), jumpsuit on hook catching different angle of dying light (more shadowed — evening coming)
Layer 6: Light in motion — sunset now reaching her more directly (she's in the shaft as it lowers to floor level), warm-orange filling her face fully, leaning mirror catching and bouncing shaft creating warm secondary bounce-light on her face from floor-angle (unique lighting configuration of floor-seated plus leaning mirror)

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Open makeup bag and palette (dark smoky shades visible in pans — charcoal, warm brown, black) on floor at her knee, slightly out of focus. Brush-holders, tissues with fallout marks.
- MIDGROUND: Aira seated, sharp focus, eye application in progress, both arms creating angular frame around face. Leaning mirror visible reflecting her back (we see her directly and reflected simultaneously).
- BACKGROUND: Empty apartment — bare wall with sunset-stripe crawling, boxes, jumpsuit on hook, curtainless window showing sunset sky now lower in frame (sunset descending). Ghost-rectangles on wall.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Sunset now flooding directly at floor level, 2600K deep amber-orange, reaching her face at direct angle, hard and warm and dramatic
- Fill: Leaning mirror bouncing sunset back at her from floor level at -1.5 stops, creating warm under-fill unique to this setup
- Rim: Golden sunset edge on right arm (elevated, hair-holding arm) catching full backlight
- Practical: Floor lamp still off. Sunset as only source.
- Light separation from BG: Subject fully in shaft now (+2 stops from shadowed walls behind her — dramatic isolation in warm light)

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video (Opening)

SHOT TYPE: Medium Shot from behind (silhouette)
CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow push-in toward her at window, 8 seconds
LENS: 35mm
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s Aira from behind, hands on window, sunset flooding. At 2.0s turns head 45 degrees (profile). At 3.5s delivers "Last sunset from this window." At 5.5s removes hands from glass (prints visible). At 7.0s turns fully toward room/camera. At 7.5s exhales, looks at room.
LIGHTING: Sunset backlighting. When she turns, sunset becomes key on face. Dramatic warm transition.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Nearly-empty apartment, curtainless window, boxes, dust in shaft. Melancholy beauty.
AUDIO: Music — Olafur Arnalds strings at -10dB, sustained violin note, piano at 3.5s. 72 BPM. Ambient — empty room reverb, city hum. SFX — at 0.0s hand-on-glass squeak, at 5.5s hands-lift-from-glass, at 7.0s bare feet on hardwood. VO — at 3.5s "Last sunset from this window." (reverent, slow, slight crack between "from" and "this").
DURATION: 8 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter.
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: At 3.5s profile delivery: "Last" L+ast. "sunset" S+un-set. "from" slight crack. "this" TH+is. "window" win-doh. Slowly, emotionally controlled.
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

# CONCEPT 26 — BEAUTY AD (Cinematic Beauty Hero)

**Product:** HAIR OIL — tall narrow amber hand-blown glass bottle (artisan asymmetric), heavy cork stopper with leather cord wrapped twice at neck, aged paper label "ELIXIR" in copper letterpress, deep golden liquid with herbal particulates suspended, weighted thick base
**Mood Archetype:** MA-6 "saffron threads dissolving in milk"
**Sub-type:** Cinematic Beauty Hero
**Duration:** 15 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x 3 seconds each
**Register:** REVERENT
**Voice:** SILENT
**Product Move:** P-3 Suspended at Apex (bottle frozen at peak of toss, motion blur on edges, trailing dust wake below)
**Camera:** Slow orbital quarter-turn around product + final pull-back to Aira
**Setting:** B-5 Atelier as AYURVEDIC SPACE (dark wood, raw herbs scattered, saffron threads, brass mortar, terracotta, cool-warm north light, clay walls, dried herb bundles hanging)
**Wardrobe:** Raw undyed cream linen wrap at one shoulder, earthy elemental
**Hair:** HC-4 Soft Hollywood but OILED and glistening (product result visible — deep shine, strands catching individual light)
**Makeup:** ML-7 Skin-First

# CONCEPT 27 — BEAUTY AD (Fragrance Mood Piece)

**Product:** SOLID PERFUME COMPACT — hand-thrown ceramic circular in matte sage-green stoneware, unglazed with potter's finger-marks (wabi-sabi), honey-glazed interior, warm amber solid formula with pressed dried flower petals in surface, brass hinge, no label — shape IS brand, thick ceramic walls suggesting weight
**Mood Archetype:** MA-29 "pressed flower preserved in resin"
**Sub-type:** Fragrance Mood Piece
**Duration:** 25 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x 5 seconds each
**Register:** TENDER
**Voice:** SILENT (single exhale at peak)
**Product Move:** P-20 Petal/Particle Gather (scattered petals attract toward compact center, converging and settling into open lid)
**Camera:** Macro push-in on compact + pull-back to Aira applying at pulse point
**Setting:** B-6 Botanical Garden (outdoor golden hour, wild lavender and chamomile, weathered wood table, dappled light through leaves, warm breeze, pollen in light)
**Wardrobe:** White cotton gauze dress, thin straps, sunlit golden skin
**Hair:** HC-23 Air-Dried Boho with golden-hour light
**Makeup:** ML-5 Effortless Day, sun-kissed
**Color Grade:** Golden hour worship, warm amber, halation, Lubezki reference, Portra 400

SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Cream oversized knit sweater visible at frame edge (Aira blurred in background). Sheer fabric (cream organza scarf on marble surface near pencil) MOVING in breeze.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Visible in background blur — HC-13 with face-framing pieces moving in same breeze.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Background — pre-liner bare lips visible in soft focus.

HAND POSITIONS: Not touching product (P-22 — pencil rests alone). Hands at body-sides in background soft-focus.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Background only — soft knowing expression barely readable in blur. Product is hero.

BODY POSTURE: Background — seated at bed-edge in soft intimate posture. Blurred.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
Layer 1: Subject micro-action — P-22 Wind-Animated Stillness: pencil rests PERFECTLY STILL on marble surface (nightstand/vanity surface) while ALL ELSE MOVES. The pencil's stillness is emphasized by surrounding motion. Its stability = product confidence. Mauve-nude tip pointing toward camera. Bamboo surface catching warm golden-hour light.
Layer 2: Fabric + hair state — sheer organza scarf on marble surface beside pencil caught in full billow from bedroom breeze (dramatic wind-movement contrasting pencil-stillness), Aira's hair in background also wind-moved (face-framing pieces drifting right), sweater-edge catching breeze
Layer 3: Particulate layer — golden-hour dust motes in bedroom shaft (15-20 particles, warm gold, drifting rightward with breeze), pollen/fiber from sheer scarf releasing into light (3-4 tiny fabric particles)
Layer 4: Contact-point activity — pencil resting on marble (only contact: pencil-barrel touching cold marble, zero-motion at contact-line, absolute stability proven), magnetic cap separate beside it (showing product ready-to-use, cap detached revealing mauve tip)
Layer 5: Background motion — golden-hour bedroom alive: sheer window-curtain billowing, warm shaft crossing space at low angle, Aira blurred and alive with breath and breeze-response, mirror camera-left catching light shifts
Layer 6: Light in motion — golden-hour shaft through bedroom window creating warm animated beam (curtain-modulated, flickering as sheer moves in-and-out of shaft), marble surface catching shifted light as curtain dances, bamboo pencil showing warm-grain-texture in golden directional light

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Marble surface with lip liner pencil (SHARP FOCUS hero), cap beside it, mauve tip visible. Sheer scarf in wind beside. The stable product in a moving world.
- MIDGROUND: Air between product and person — golden dust in shaft, breeze visible.

FRAMING: Product hero with environmental context — pencil at center-frame on marble, scarf and background Aira creating alive frame. Product 30% of frame height, precisely centered.

LENS: 65mm. APERTURE: f/2.8 — pencil sharp, sheer scarf in moderate motion-blur, background Aira soft. Bokeh: round, warm golden.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Still-life-in-motion — product photography meets cinematic environment. The pencil as calm center in golden storm.

### Full Sequence — Video (20 seconds)

SHOT TYPE: ECU (lips) + pull-back to MCU
CAMERA MOVEMENT: 0-3s: static on product (wind-animated still life). 3-4s: transition to ECU lips. 4-14s: ECU STATIC on lips during full application. 14-16s: slow pull-back from ECU to MCU. 16-20s: MCU static for knowing-look and sign-off.
LENS: 100mm macro (ECU) rack to 50mm (MCU)
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s product resting with wind around it. At 3.0s cut/transition to ECU on lips. At 4.0s "Cupid's bow first..." — pencil draws V at upper lip (visible application). At 7.0s "...then corners..." — pencil moves to right corner, then left. At 10.0s "now just..." — pencil connecting upper-lip line. At 11.5s "...connect." — lower lip lined (connection complete). At 14.0s camera pulls back. At 16.0s full face visible, knowing expression, touch-testing lip. At 18.0s "Samajh gayi?" — direct address with knowing brow-raise.
LIGHTING: Golden-hour bedroom throughout. Warm shaft on lips during ECU creating texture-visibility. Pull-back revealing full golden-room context.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Golden-hour bedroom, bed-edge, mirror, sheer in breeze. Intimate warm tutorial space.
AUDIO: Music — lo-fi warm keys at -10dB, intimate bedroom-tutorial soundtrack, 88 BPM gentle. Ambient — soft breeze, fabric-sheer movement, intimate room quiet. SFX — at 0.0s wind-on-fabric whoosh (sheer moving), at 4.0s pencil-on-lip (barely audible, intimate tactile ASMR-adjacent), at 11.5s lip-press (lips pressing together testing line — satisfying). VO — at 4.0s "Cupid's bow first..." (knowing, intimate teacher voice, close-mic, instructional but sexy). At 7.0s "...then corners..." (slightly softer). At 10.0s "now just..." (trailing, building). At 11.5s "...connect." (satisfied, definitive, slight smile in voice). At 18.0s "Samajh gayi?" (Hindi — "Got it?" — delivered with raised brow energy, playful, warm, knowing wink in voice without actual wink).
DURATION: 20 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, ECU static shows zero blur during precision application (maximum sharpness for tutorial clarity).
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: At 4.0s "Cupid's" — K-yoo-pidz (lips form around words while being lined — dual-action). "bow" — B-oh. "first" — F-irst. At 7.0s "then" — TH-en. "corners" — K-or-nerz. At 10.0s "now" — N-ow. "just" — J-ust. At 11.5s "connect" — K-uh-NEKT (slight emphasis on final syllable). At 18.0s "Samajh" — S-uh-MAHJ. "gayi?" — GUY-ee (rising questioning intonation, brow-raise accompanies). Lips visible throughout ECU — dual challenge of speaking and liner-application simultaneously (authentic to content-creator technique).
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

# CONCEPT 30 — BEAUTY AD (Beauty Editorial Film)

**Product:** BODY SHIMMER OIL — tall slim clear glass bottle, visible golden oil with suspended micro-gold-flecks, brushed brass pump, elongated elegant silhouette, clean serif "LUMIERE" in gold foil on transparent label, weighted teardrop base, golden caustic refraction through glass
**Mood Archetype:** MA-17 "the gleam beneath polished surfaces"
**Sub-type:** Beauty Editorial Film
**Duration:** 30 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 5 seconds each
**Register:** REVERENT
**Voice:** SILENT
**Product Move:** P-7 Gravity-Free Pour (golden oil exits pump in curving ribbon mid-air, surface tension holding arc before landing on collarbone)
**Camera:** Vertical tilt collarbone-to-face + parallax slide final
**Setting:** B-8 INDOOR INFINITY POOL AT SUNSET (still water reflecting gold sunset, marble pool edge, warm steam, Aira at edge legs in water, floor-to-ceiling glass wall flooding golden hour)
**Wardrobe:** Champagne silk sarong-wrap at torso, legs bare mid-thigh into water, body shimmer already on legs/shoulders (glistening), bare feet in warm water
**Hair:** HC-4 Soft Hollywood slightly damp at ends, golden highlights extreme
**Makeup:** ML-3 Clean Editorial + extreme collarbone/cheekbone highlight from body shimmer
**Color Grade:** Extreme golden-hour amber, highlights warm-white blown, shadows warm bronze, skin inner-glow, halation, Lubezki golden worship, Fuji Eterna

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Full Sequence — Video (30 seconds)

SHOT TYPE: Vertical tilt + parallax slide
CAMERA MOVEMENT: 0-5s: macro on product-pour (P-7 oil-ribbon). 5-15s: slow vertical tilt from collarbone upward to face (ascending over shimmer-applied body). 15-25s: slow push-in on face (shimmer-result reveal on cheekbones). 25-30s: parallax slide rightward revealing pool-and-sunset-world in background (final editorial-film establishing depth).
LENS: 65mm for body-detail, transitioning to 50mm for face
SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s product pump depressed, oil-ribbon exits in arc toward collarbone. At 2.0s oil lands, golden spread begins. At 5.0s camera begins tilting up — hand spreading shimmer visible at collarbone. At 8.0s shoulders visible, glistening. At 11.0s neck and jaw enter frame (shimmer on neck visible). At 13.0s face enters — half-lidded pleasure. At 15.0s push-in begins on face (shimmer-result at cheekbones catching golden light in constellation). At 20.0s eyes open fully (direct camera address — reverent). At 22.0s she raises bottle to frame-edge (product visible with her). At 25.0s parallax slide begins (camera moves right, revealing pool, sunset, golden world behind her). At 28.0s full editorial frame — her in golden pool-world with product. At 30.0s holds. End.
LIGHTING: Extreme golden-hour through floor-to-ceiling glass + pool-reflection from below. Shimmer-on-skin as self-illuminating. Maximum golden everywhere. Unified amber world.
ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Indoor infinity pool at sunset. Marble edge. Still water reflecting golden sky. Warm steam rising. Floor-to-ceiling glass flooding amber. Maximum luxury golden-hour.
AUDIO: Music — cinematic ambient strings + warm electronic pad at -6dB, swelling slowly through 30 seconds to emotional peak at 25s (parallax reveal of golden world). No beat — pure atmosphere. Ambient — pool water gentle (small ripple sounds, therapeutic), warm steam whisper. SFX — at 0.0s pump-click (brass mechanical, satisfying, precise), at 0.0s oil-exit-from-nozzle (liquid-flow beginning), at 2.0s oil-landing-on-skin (golden-wet-contact, intimate ASMR), at 5.0s hand-spreading-on-skin (smooth gliding sound, zero-friction from oil), throughout: pool-water-ambient and steam creating cocoon of warm sound. VO — none (SILENT — 30 seconds of pure visual poetry).
DURATION: 30 seconds
FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, vertical tilt smooth and cinematic, parallax slide creating beautiful depth-separation between subject and background.
LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: No lip movement throughout entire 30 seconds. Lips in soft neutral at pleasure-rest throughout. At 20.0s slight parting for soft exhale (non-verbal, pleasure only). SILENT beauty editorial — no words, only gold.
NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.
